N\+M\+EA sentences Bit Mask indicating the N\+M\+EA sentences enabled in the N\+M\+EA flow.

Add handler function for E\+V\+E\+NT \textquotesingle{}le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Position\textquotesingle{}

This event provides information on position.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item A handler reference, which is only needed for later removal of the handler.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Doesn\textquotesingle{}t return on failure, so there\textquotesingle{}s no need to check the return value for errors. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\index{le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+interface.\+h}!le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Connect\+Service@{le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Connect\+Service}}
\index{le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Connect\+Service@{le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Connect\+Service}!le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+interface.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Connect\+Service(void)}{le_gnss_ConnectService(void)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Connect\+Service (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{void}]{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\hypertarget{le__gnss__interface_8h_a3b352251c2764092c56f20592f5894ca}{}\label{le__gnss__interface_8h_a3b352251c2764092c56f20592f5894ca}
Connect the current client thread to the service providing this A\+PI. Block until the service is available.

For each thread that wants to use this A\+PI, either Connect\+Service or Try\+Connect\+Service must be called before any other functions in this A\+PI. Normally, Connect\+Service is automatically called for the main thread, but not for any other thread. For details, see \hyperlink{apiFilesC_apiFilesC_client}{Client-\/specific Functions}.

This function is created automatically. \index{le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+interface.\+h}!le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Delete\+Supl\+Certificate@{le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Delete\+Supl\+Certificate}}

\index{le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Disconnect\+Service@{le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Disconnect\+Service}!le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+interface.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Disconnect\+Service(void)}{le_gnss_DisconnectService(void)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Disconnect\+Service (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{void}]{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\hypertarget{le__gnss__interface_8h_aeb249461b02547251a5b5e1e8bb28a95}{}\label{le__gnss__interface_8h_aeb249461b02547251a5b5e1e8bb28a95}
Disconnect the current client thread from the service providing this A\+PI.

Normally, this function doesn\textquotesingle{}t need to be called. After this function is called, there\textquotesingle{}s no longer a connection to the service, and the functions in this A\+PI can\textquotesingle{}t be used. For details, see \hyperlink{apiFilesC_apiFilesC_client}{Client-\/specific Functions}.

This function is created automatically. \index{le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+interface.\+h}!le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Enable@{le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Enable}}

\index{le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Get\+Altitude@{le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Get\+Altitude}!le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+interface.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Get\+Altitude(le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Sample\+Ref\+\_\+t position\+Sample\+Ref, int32\+\_\+t $\ast$altitude\+Ptr, int32\+\_\+t $\ast$v\+Accuracy\+Ptr)}{le_gnss_GetAltitude(le_gnss_SampleRef_t positionSampleRef, int32_t *altitudePtr, int32_t *vAccuracyPtr)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf le\+\_\+result\+\_\+t} le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Get\+Altitude (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Sample\+Ref\+\_\+t}}]{position\+Sample\+Ref, }
\item[{int32\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{altitude\+Ptr, }
\item[{int32\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{v\+Accuracy\+Ptr}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\hypertarget{le__gnss__interface_8h_a5cc278268a4e75c5e2a5f8c1ffb64fa9}{}\label{le__gnss__interface_8h_a5cc278268a4e75c5e2a5f8c1ffb64fa9}
Get the position sample\textquotesingle{}s altitude.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+F\+A\+U\+LT Function failed to get the altitude. Invalid Position reference provided.
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+\_\+\+O\+F\+\_\+\+R\+A\+N\+GE One of the retrieved parameter is invalid (set to I\+N\+T32\+\_\+\+M\+AX).
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+OK Function succeeded.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Altitude is in meters, above Mean Sea Level, with 3 decimal places (3047 = 3.\+047 meters).

For a 2D position fix, the altitude will be indicated as invalid and set to I\+N\+T32\+\_\+\+M\+AX

Vertical position accuracy is in meters with 1 decimal places (3047 = 3.\+0 meters).

If the caller is passing an invalid Position reference into this function, it is a fatal error, the function will not return.

altitude\+Ptr, altitude\+Accuracy\+Ptr can be set to N\+U\+LL if not needed. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em position\+Sample\+Ref} & Position sample\textquotesingle{}s reference. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em altitude\+Ptr} & Altitude in meters, above Mean Sea Level \mbox{[}resolution 1e-\/3\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em v\+Accuracy\+Ptr} & Vertical position\textquotesingle{}s accuracy in meters \mbox{[}resolution 1e-\/1\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Get the position sample\textquotesingle{}s altitude with respect to the W\+G\+S-\/84 ellipsoid

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+F\+A\+U\+LT Function failed to get the altitude.
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+\_\+\+O\+F\+\_\+\+R\+A\+N\+GE One of the retrieved parameter is invalid (set to I\+N\+T32\+\_\+\+M\+AX).
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+OK Function succeeded.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
altitude\+On\+Wgs84 is in meters, with respect to the W\+G\+S-\/84 ellipsoid with 3 decimal places (3047 = 3.\+047 meters).

For a 2D position fix, the altitude with respect to the W\+G\+S-\/84 ellipsoid will be indicated as invalid and set to I\+N\+T32\+\_\+\+M\+AX.

If the caller is passing an invalid Position reference into this function, it is a fatal error, the function will not return. 
\end{DoxyNote}

Get the D\+OP parameter (Dilution Of Precision) for the fixed position.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+F\+A\+U\+LT Function failed to find the D\+OP value.
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+\_\+\+O\+F\+\_\+\+R\+A\+N\+GE The retrieved parameter is invalid (set to U\+I\+N\+T16\+\_\+\+M\+AX).
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+OK Function succeeded.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This function replaces the deprecated function \hyperlink{le__gnss__interface_8h_a70504e7c542d626aa07948d8330020c7}{le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Get\+Dop()}.

The D\+OP value is given with 3 decimal places by default like\+: D\+OP value 2200 = 2.\+200 The resolution can be modified by calling the {\ttfamily \hyperlink{le__gnss__interface_8h_ae7345052efc38f199989aafcd27224e2}{le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Set\+Dop\+Resolution()}} function.

If the caller is passing an invalid Position sample reference into this function, it is a fatal error, the function will not return. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em position\+Sample\+Ref} & Position sample\textquotesingle{}s reference. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em dop\+Type} & Dilution of Precision type. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em dop\+Ptr} & Dilution of Precision corresponding to the dop\+Type \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Get the position sample\textquotesingle{}s direction. Direction of movement is the direction that the vehicle or person is actually moving.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+F\+A\+U\+LT Function failed to find the position\+Sample.
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+\_\+\+O\+F\+\_\+\+R\+A\+N\+GE One of the retrieved parameter is invalid (set to U\+I\+N\+T32\+\_\+\+M\+AX).
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+OK Function succeeded.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Direction and direction accuracy are given in degrees with 1 decimal place\+: 1755 = 175.\+5 degrees. Direction ranges from 0 to 359.\+9 degrees, where 0 is True North.

direction\+Ptr, direction\+Accuracy\+Ptr can be set to N\+U\+LL if not needed.

If the caller is passing an invalid Position sample reference into this function, it is a fatal error, the function will not return. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em direction\+Accuracy\+Ptr} & Direction\textquotesingle{}s accuracy estimate in degrees \mbox{[}resolution 1e-\/1\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Get\+Gps\+Leap\+Seconds(le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Sample\+Ref\+\_\+t position\+Sample\+Ref, uint8\+\_\+t $\ast$leap\+Seconds\+Ptr)}{le_gnss_GetGpsLeapSeconds(le_gnss_SampleRef_t positionSampleRef, uint8_t *leapSecondsPtr)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf le\+\_\+result\+\_\+t} le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Get\+Gps\+Leap\+Seconds (

Get the position sample\textquotesingle{}s U\+TC leap seconds in advance

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+F\+A\+U\+LT Function failed to get the leap seconds.
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+\_\+\+O\+F\+\_\+\+R\+A\+N\+GE The retrieved time accuracy is invalid (set to U\+I\+N\+T8\+\_\+\+M\+AX).
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+OK Function succeeded.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The leap seconds in advance is the accumulated time in seconds since the start of G\+PS Epoch time (Jan 6, 1980). This value has to be added to the U\+TC time (since Jan. 1, 1970)

Insertion of each U\+TC leap second is usually decided about six months in advance by the International Earth Rotation and Reference Systems Service (I\+E\+RS).

If the caller is passing an invalid position sample reference or a null pointer into this function, it is a fatal error, the function will not return. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em position\+Sample\+Ref} & Position sample\textquotesingle{}s reference. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em leap\+Seconds\+Ptr} & U\+TC leap seconds in advance in seconds \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyParamCaption}

Get the position sample\textquotesingle{}s horizontal speed.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+F\+A\+U\+LT Function failed to find the position\+Sample.
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+\_\+\+O\+F\+\_\+\+R\+A\+N\+GE One of the retrieved parameter is invalid (set to U\+I\+N\+T32\+\_\+\+M\+AX).
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+OK Function succeeded.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
h\+Speed\+Ptr, h\+Speed\+Accuracy\+Ptr can be set to N\+U\+LL if not needed.

Horizontal speed is in meters/second with 2 decimal places (3047 = 30.\+47 meters/second).

Horizontal speed accuracy estimate is in meters/second with 1 decimal place (304 = 30.\+4 meters/second).

If the caller is passing an invalid Position sample reference into this function, it is a fatal error, the function will not return.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
The Horizontal speed accuracy is platform dependent. Please refer to \hyperlink{platformConstraintsGnss_platformConstraintsGnss_speedAccuracies}{Horizontal and Vertical speed accuracies} section for full details. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em hspeed\+Accuracy\+Ptr} & Horizontal speed\textquotesingle{}s accuracy estimate in meters/second \mbox{[}resolution 1e-\/1\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\item[{{\bf le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Sample\+Ref\+\_\+t}}]{position\+Sample\+Ref, }
\item[{int32\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{latitude\+Ptr, }
\item[{int32\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{longitude\+Ptr, }
\item[{int32\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{h\+Accuracy\+Ptr}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\hypertarget{le__gnss__interface_8h_ada100f53f9ad9f3df852fcc6639c15bc}{}\label{le__gnss__interface_8h_ada100f53f9ad9f3df852fcc6639c15bc}
Get the location\textquotesingle{}s data (Latitude, Longitude, Horizontal accuracy).

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+F\+A\+U\+LT Function failed to get the location\textquotesingle{}s data
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+\_\+\+O\+F\+\_\+\+R\+A\+N\+GE One of the retrieved parameter is invalid (set to I\+N\+T32\+\_\+\+M\+AX).
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+OK Function succeeded.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
latitude\+Ptr, longitude\+Ptr and h\+Accuracy\+Ptr can be set to N\+U\+LL if not needed.

The latitude and longitude values are based on the W\+G\+S84 standard coordinate system.

The latitude and longitude values are given in degrees with 6 decimal places like\+: Latitude +48858300 = 48.\+858300 degrees North Longitude +2294400 = 2.\+294400 degrees East (The latitude and longitude values are given in degrees, minutes, seconds in N\+M\+EA frame)

If the caller is passing an invalid Position sample reference into this function, it is a fatal error, the function will not return. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em position\+Sample\+Ref} & Position sample\textquotesingle{}s reference. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em latitude\+Ptr} & W\+G\+S84 Latitude in degrees, positive North \mbox{[}resolution 1e-\/6\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em longitude\+Ptr} & W\+G\+S84 Longitude in degrees, positive East \mbox{[}resolution 1e-\/6\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em h\+Accuracy\+Ptr} & Horizontal position\textquotesingle{}s accuracy in meters \mbox{[}resolution 1e-\/2\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Get the position sample\textquotesingle{}s magnetic deviation. It is the difference between the bearing to true north and the bearing shown on a magnetic compass. The deviation is positive when the magnetic north is east of true north.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+F\+A\+U\+LT Function failed to find the position\+Sample.
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+\_\+\+O\+F\+\_\+\+R\+A\+N\+GE One of the retrieved parameter is invalid (set to I\+N\+T32\+\_\+\+M\+AX).
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+OK Function succeeded.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
magnetic\+Deviation is in degrees, with 1 decimal places (47 = 4.\+7 degree).

If the caller is passing an invalid Position sample reference into this function, it is a fatal error, the function will not return. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}

Get the Satellites Vehicle information.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+F\+A\+U\+LT Function failed to find the position\+Sample.
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+\_\+\+O\+F\+\_\+\+R\+A\+N\+GE One of the retrieved parameter is invalid.
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+OK Function succeeded.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
sat\+Id\mbox{[}\mbox{]} can be set to 0 if that information list index is not configured, so all satellite parameters (sat\+Const\mbox{[}\mbox{]}, sat\+Snr\mbox{[}\mbox{]},sat\+Azim\mbox{[}\mbox{]}, sat\+Elev\mbox{[}\mbox{]}) are fixed to 0.

For L\+E\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+\_\+\+O\+F\+\_\+\+R\+A\+N\+GE returned code, invalid value depends on field type\+: U\+I\+N\+T16\+\_\+\+M\+AX for sat\+Id, L\+E\+\_\+\+G\+N\+S\+S\+\_\+\+S\+V\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+S\+T\+E\+L\+L\+A\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+U\+N\+D\+E\+F\+I\+N\+ED for sat\+Const, false for sat\+Used, U\+I\+N\+T8\+\_\+\+M\+AX for sat\+Snr, U\+I\+N\+T16\+\_\+\+M\+AX for sat\+Azim, U\+I\+N\+T8\+\_\+\+M\+AX for sat\+Elev.

If the caller is passing an invalid Position sample reference into this function, it is a fatal error, the function will not return. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em sat\+Azim\+Ptr} & Satellites in View Azimuth \mbox{[}degrees\mbox{]}. Range\+: 0 to 360 If Azimuth angle is currently unknown, the value is set to U\+I\+N\+T16\+\_\+\+M\+AX. \\

Get the position sample\textquotesingle{}s vertical speed.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+F\+A\+U\+LT The function failed to find the position\+Sample.
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+\_\+\+O\+F\+\_\+\+R\+A\+N\+GE One of the retrieved parameter is not valid (set to I\+N\+T32\+\_\+\+M\+AX).
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+OK The function succeeded.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
v\+Speed\+Ptr, v\+Speed\+Accuracy\+Ptr can be set to N\+U\+LL if not needed.

For a 2D position Fix, the vertical speed will be indicated as invalid and set to I\+N\+T32\+\_\+\+M\+AX.

If the caller is passing an invalid Position sample reference into this function, it is a fatal error, the function will not return.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
The Vertical speed accuracy is platform dependent. Please refer to \hyperlink{platformConstraintsGnss_platformConstraintsGnss_speedAccuracies}{Horizontal and Vertical speed accuracies} section for full details. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em position\+Sample\+Ref} & Position sample\textquotesingle{}s reference. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em vspeed\+Ptr} & Vertical speed in meters/second \mbox{[}resolution 1e-\/2\mbox{]}, positive up. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em vspeed\+Accuracy\+Ptr} & Vertical speed\textquotesingle{}s accuracy estimate in meters/second \mbox{[}resolution 1e-\/1\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\index{le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Inject\+Supl\+Certificate@{le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Inject\+Supl\+Certificate}!le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+interface.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Inject\+Supl\+Certificate(uint8\+\_\+t supl\+Certificate\+Id, uint16\+\_\+t supl\+Certificate\+Len, const char $\ast$\+L\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+N\+N\+U\+L\+L supl\+Certificate)}{le_gnss_InjectSuplCertificate(uint8_t suplCertificateId, uint16_t suplCertificateLen, const char *LE_NONNULL suplCertificate)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf le\+\_\+result\+\_\+t} le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Inject\+Supl\+Certificate (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{supl\+Certificate\+Id, }
\item[{uint16\+\_\+t}]{supl\+Certificate\+Len, }
\item[{const char $\ast$L\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+N\+N\+U\+LL}]{supl\+Certificate}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\hypertarget{le__gnss__interface_8h_a85bda68acc951ee14f5678dd8d1b532f}{}\label{le__gnss__interface_8h_a85bda68acc951ee14f5678dd8d1b532f}
This function injects the S\+U\+PL certificate to be used in A-\/\+G\+N\+SS sessions. Certificates must be encoded in D\+ER. Other certificate encryptions (e.\+g., P\+EM, C\+ER and C\+RT) aren\textquotesingle{}t supported.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+OK on success
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+B\+A\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER on invalid parameter
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+F\+A\+U\+LT on failure
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+B\+U\+SY service is busy
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+T\+I\+M\+E\+O\+UT a time-\/out occurred
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If the S\+U\+PL certificate size is bigger than the Maximum S\+U\+PL certificate size, it is a fatal error, the function will not return. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em supl\+Certificate\+Id} & ID of the S\+U\+PL certificate. Certificate ID range is 0 to 9 \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em supl\+Certificate\+Len} & S\+U\+PL certificate size in Bytes. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em supl\+Certificate} & S\+U\+PL certificate contents. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

This function sets the G\+N\+SS device acquisition rate.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+OK on success
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+F\+A\+U\+LT on failure
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+U\+N\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+R\+T\+ED request not supported
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+T\+I\+M\+E\+O\+UT a time-\/out occurred
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+P\+E\+R\+M\+I\+T\+T\+ED If the G\+N\+SS device is not in \char`\"{}ready\char`\"{} state.
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+O\+U\+T\+\_\+\+O\+F\+\_\+\+R\+A\+N\+GE if acquisition rate value is equal to zero
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
This function may be subject to limitations depending on the platform. Please refer to the \hyperlink{platformConstraintsGnss}{G\+N\+SS platform constraints} page.

The settings are platform dependent. Please refer to \hyperlink{platformConstraintsGnss_platformConstraintsGnss_SettingConfiguration}{Setting configuration} section for full details.

\index{le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Set\+Supl\+Server\+Url@{le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Set\+Supl\+Server\+Url}!le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+interface.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Set\+Supl\+Server\+Url(const char $\ast$\+L\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+N\+N\+U\+L\+L supl\+Server\+Url)}{le_gnss_SetSuplServerUrl(const char *LE_NONNULL suplServerUrl)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf le\+\_\+result\+\_\+t} le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Set\+Supl\+Server\+Url (

This function sets the S\+U\+PL server U\+RL. That server U\+RL is a N\+U\+L\+L-\/terminated string with a maximum string length (including N\+U\+LL terminator) equal to 256. Optionally the port number is specified after a colon.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+OK on success
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+F\+A\+U\+LT on failure
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+B\+U\+SY service is busy
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+T\+I\+M\+E\+O\+UT a time-\/out occurred
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If the S\+U\+PL server U\+RL size is bigger than the maximum string length (including N\+U\+LL terminator) size, it is a fatal error, the function will not return.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
The settings are platform dependent. Please refer to \hyperlink{platformConstraintsGnss_platformConstraintsGnss_SettingConfiguration}{Setting configuration} section for full details. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em supl\+Server\+Url} & S\+U\+PL server U\+RL. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\index{le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+interface.\+h}!le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Try\+Connect\+Service@{le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Try\+Connect\+Service}}
\index{le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Try\+Connect\+Service@{le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Try\+Connect\+Service}!le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+interface.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Try\+Connect\+Service(void)}{le_gnss_TryConnectService(void)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf le\+\_\+result\+\_\+t} le\+\_\+gnss\+\_\+\+Try\+Connect\+Service (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{void}]{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\hypertarget{le__gnss__interface_8h_ab73c2f8ce9e85d774d44b95b4f4a8637}{}\label{le__gnss__interface_8h_ab73c2f8ce9e85d774d44b95b4f4a8637}
Try to connect the current client thread to the service providing this A\+PI. Return with an error if the service is not available.

For each thread that wants to use this A\+PI, either Connect\+Service or Try\+Connect\+Service must be called before any other functions in this A\+PI. Normally, Connect\+Service is automatically called for the main thread, but not for any other thread. For details, see \hyperlink{apiFilesC_apiFilesC_client}{Client-\/specific Functions}.

This function is created automatically.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+OK if the client connected successfully to the service.
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+U\+N\+A\+V\+A\+I\+L\+A\+B\+LE if the server is not currently offering the service to which the client is bound.
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+P\+E\+R\+M\+I\+T\+T\+ED if the client interface is not bound to any service (doesn\textquotesingle{}t have a binding).
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+M\+M\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR if the Service Directory cannot be reached. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
